		, ".\\test.mdl" = as.character(c(
			  " test()  "
			, "  { "
			, "  deriv(Aa = - Ka * Aa)"
			, "  deriv(A1 = Ka * Aa + K21*A2 - K12*A1 + K31*A3 - K12*A2 - Vmax * C **GAMMA/ (Km **GAMMA + C **GAMMA))"
			, "  deriv(A2 = K12 * A1 - K21*A2) "
			, "  deriv(A3 = K13 * A1 - K31*A3)"
			, "  fixef(GAMMA= c(0.0001, 1.6, 3 ))  "
			, "  C = A1 / V"
			, "  dosepoint(Aa, idosevar = AaDose, infdosevar = AaInfDose, infratevar =  AaInfRate)"
			, "  error(CEps = 0.5) "
			, "  observe(CObs=C + CEps * sqrt(1 + C^2 * (CMultStdev/sigma())^2)) "
			, "  fixef( CMultStdev = c(0,1,))"
			, "  stparm(Vmax = tvVmax * exp( nVmax ))"
			, "  fixef(tvVmax= c(100, 4000, ))  "
			, "  stparm(Km = tvKm * exp( nV ))"
			, "  fixef(tvKm= c(100, 4000, ))  "
			, "  fcovariate(WT)"
			, "  stparm(V = tvV *(WT/70)^dVdWT * exp( nKm ))"
			, "  fixef(tvV= c(1, 50, )) "
			, "  stparm(Ka = tvKa )"
			, "  fixef(tvKa= c(0.01, 1.2, 3))   "
			, "  fixef(K12= c(0.0001, 2, 10 ))"
			, "  fixef(K21= c(0.0001, 3, 10 ))  "
			, "  fixef(K13= c(0.0001, 0.1, 10 ))"
			, "  fixef(K31= c(0.0001, 0.05, 10 )) "
			, "  ranef(diag(nVmax,nKm,nV) = c(0.31,0.31,0.31))"
			, "  fixef(dVdWT=c(0, 1.1, 10 ))  "
			, "  }"
			))
		, "cols1.txt" = as.character(c(
			  "id(\"ID\")"
			, "time(\"TIME\")"
			, "dose(Aa<-\"AMT\")"
			, "covr(WT<-\"WT\")"
			, "obs(CObs<-\"IOBS\")"
			, "table(file=\"posthoc.csv\", covr(WT), Vmax, Km, V, Ka, mode=keep)"
			, ""
			))
		)
	, names = c("coefficients", "logLik", "nObs", "nSubj", "nParm", "returnCode", "omega", "eta", "eta_shrinkage", "sigma", "method", "varFix", "omegaSE", "Covariance", "Correlation", "Inverse", "LLTable", "residuals", "posthoc", ".\\test.mdl", "cols1.txt")
	, class = "nlme"
